**Task:** Review trading performance and propose profit‑maximizing changes; output JSON with `recommendations`, `already_implemented`, `rejected` (with reasons).

**Data gathered:**
1. **Trade insights (blofin_get_trade_insights)**
   - Strategy: “big winners pay for small losers” → favor symbols with large avg_win & total PnL; skip symbols with ≥3 losses; never clip winners; never add to blocked positions.
   - Symbol stats: *All* listed symbols have 0 wins, negative total PnL; many have 1–5 losses. Notable losses: RESOLV‑USDT (‑0.338 USDT, 5 losses), BLESS‑USDT (‑0.074 USDT, 4 losses), BTC‑USDT (‑0.0118 USDT, 1 loss). No positive PnL symbols.
   - Recent events (last ~10 min):
     - Orders placed: GOAT‑USDT (buy), ADA‑USDT (buy → blocked), STABLE‑USDT (sell), WLD‑USDT (sell).
     - Positions closed (losses): GWEI‑USDT, AIGENSYN‑USDT, MON‑USDT, JUP‑USDT.
     - Blocked order: ADA‑USDT (already open long).

2. **Learned tactics (blofin_get_learned_tactics)**
   - 15+ **SELF‑HEAL** rules already active (repair missing TP/SL, handle API 429 TPSL rate‑limit, restart dashboard/server, clear stale caches, avoid adding size to symbols with open positions, etc.). **Already implemented** – no changes needed.
   - Recent cycle candidates (risk flags):
     - Risk‑free (risk=False): **GUN‑USDT** (Cycle 4), **UB‑USDT** (Cycles 1‑2), **TAC‑USDT** (Cycle 2).
     - Risk‑true (risk=True): other candidates (ZORA‑USDT, TOSHI‑USDT, JUP‑USDT, ADA‑USDT, etc.) – rejected by risk manager.
   - Issues:
     - TPSL rate‑limit (HTTP 429) affecting symbols: AVAAI‑USDT, GUN‑USDT, USELESS‑USDT, BOME‑USDT, NOM‑USDT.
     - Dashboard server not listening (port 7878) – self‑heal will restart.
     - Stale position cache & account data – self‑heal refreshes.

3. **Overall assessment**
   - Portfolio currently **loss‑only**; no winning trades recorded.
   - Many symbols are **blocked** (e.g., VELVET‑USDT, ADA‑USDT, GOAT‑USDT) or have high block counts.
   - Recent trades resulted in small losses; stop‑losses were tight (≈1 %); take‑profits set around 2.5 % (default) – below the desired ≥5 % target for 4:1+ R:R.
   - Risk parameters: stop ≈ 1‑1.2 % from entry; TP ≥ 5‑10 % (aim for 5:1+ reward‑to‑risk).

**Recommendations (to be placed in JSON):**
1. **Filter universe:** Exclude symbols with ≥3 losses or high block counts; keep only risk‑free recent candidates (UB‑USDT, TAC‑USDT, GUN‑USDT if 429 cleared).
2. **Validate 24 h price move & volume** for those candidates (use ranking API) to ensure “explosive move + real volume” before entry.
3. **Adjust TP/SL defaults:** Set TP = 5‑10 % (or higher) and SL = 1‑1.2 % to meet ≥4:1 R:R; override default 2.5 %/1.5 % if needed.
4. **Pre‑trade position check:** Verify no open position on the symbol before placing an order to avoid “order blocked” errors (already covered by self‑heal but can be pre‑checked).
5. **Monitor TPSL rate‑limit:** If API returns 429 for a chosen symbol (e.g., GUN‑USDT), allow self‑heal to skip TPSL veto and set TP/SL manually after recovery.
6. **Maintain self‑heal playbook:** No changes required; all listed self‑heal tactics are active and proven.

**Already implemented (no action needed):**
- All SELF‑HEAL tactics (missing TP/SL repair, rate‑limit handling, dashboard restart, stale cache refresh, etc.).
- Tight stop‑loss (≈1 %) and default TP (2.5 %) logic (though TP needs raising per recommendation).
- Blocking of orders when a position already exists (as seen with ADA‑USDT).

**Rejected proposals (with reasons):**
- “Increase position size on symbols with any loss” → violates core doctrine (big winners must cover small losers) and risk manager flags.
- “Remove all block checks” → would cause repeated order rejections and potential over‑exposure; self‑heal already handles safely.
- “Set TP to 2 % (lower than current) to capture quick wins” → reduces reward‑to‑risk below required 4:1, contrary to profit‑maximizing goal.

### Profit-Strategist-Agent — 2026-07-01T17:40:39.993181

**Summary of Current State**

- The portfolio is currently loss‑only; no winning trades have been recorded.
- Recent trades used the default TP = 2.5 % and SL ≈ 1.5 %, giving a reward‑to‑risk well below the required ≥ 4:1 (ideally ≥ 5:1) for asymmetric payoff.
- Journal shows many symbols with multiple losses and **zero** positive total PnL.  
  Examples: `RESOLV‑USDT` (‑0.338 USDT, 5 losses), `BLESS‑USDT` (‑0.074 USDT, 4 losses), `BTC‑USDT` (‑0.0118 USDT, 1 loss).  
  No symbols have a net positive PnL or a high average win.
- Several symbols are **blocked** because a position already exists (`ADA‑USDT`, `GOAT‑USDT`, etc.).
- Self‑heal playbook already contains 15+ rules handling missing TP/SL, API‑429 rate‑limit, dashboard restarts, cache refreshes, and pre‑trade position checks.
- The ranking API (`blofin_rank_opportunities`) can filter symbols by 24 h momentum, volume, and journal performance, but it is not currently being used to enforce the “explosive move + real volume” rule before entry.
- Current risk parameters (default) are:  
  - **Stop‑loss** ≈ 1‑1.2 % (good)  
  - **Take‑profit** ≈ 2.5 % (too low for the profit doctrine.

**Hypotheses / Possible Improvements**

1. **Raise default TP** to ≥ 5 % (or 5‑10 %) while keeping SL at 1‑1.2 % to achieve ≥ 4:1 R:R.
2. **Tighten symbol selection**: filter out any instrument with ≥ 3 recorded losses or total PnL ≤ 0, and only consider symbols that the ranking API flags as having > 5 % 24 h price change **and** high volume.
3. **Add a “minimum avg_win” filter** – require avg_win ≥ 5 % before a symbol can be entered.
4. **Introduce a “max_concurrent_positions” cap** (e.g., ≤ 3) to avoid over‑exposure and keep the portfolio lean for big winners.
5. **Automate TP/SL re‑evaluation** after entry: if the market moves > 2 % in‑flight, keep the TP unchanged (do not clip) and let the stop trail at 1 % to lock in profit.
6. **Expose the new parameters as environment variables** (`OWL_TP_PCT`, `OWL_SL_PCT`, `OWL_MIN_CHG24H`, `OWL_MAX_LOSSES`, `OWL_MIN_AVG_WIN`) so ops can tweak without code changes.

**Evaluation**

- Hypotheses 1, 2, 3, 5, 6 directly address the profit doctrine (asymmetric payoff, large winners, avoid early clipping, focus on explosive moves).  
- Hypothesis 4 is a safety guard but could limit upside; it is optional and can be set high (e.g., 5) to avoid unnecessary restriction.  
- All proposed changes are **not** already present in the self‑heal playbook; they require new configuration/tuning.

**Chosen Actions**

Implement the following concrete, verifiable changes:

| Change | Reason | Expected Impact | Implement |
|--------|--------|----------------|-----------|
| Set `OWL_TP_PCT = 7` (default TP = 7 %) | Gives 5‑10 % typical target, meeting ≥ 4:1 R:R with SL ≈ 1.2 % | Larger profit per winning trade; aligns with profit doctrine | true |
| Set `OWL_SL_PCT = 1.1` (default SL = 1.1 %) | Tight stop to limit loss size | Keeps losers small & fast | true |
| Introduce `OWL_MAX_LOSSES = 2` (exclude symbols with ≥ 3 recorded losses) | Removes repeatedly losing instruments | Improves win‑bias, focuses on high‑potential symbols | true |
| Introduce `OWL_MIN_CHG24H = 5` (require ≥ 5 % 24 h price change) | Ensures “explosive move” criterion | Higher probability of strong directional momentum | true |
| Introduce `OWL_MIN_AVG_WIN = 5` (require avg win ≥ 5 %) | Filters for symbols that have historically delivered large winners | Increases chance of asymmetric payoff | true |
| Add pre‑trade filter using `blofin_rank_opportunities` with `side=any`, `top_n=20` and apply the above thresholds before order placement | Guarantees volume & momentum backing | Reduces false entries, improves win rate | true |
| Keep existing self‑heal tactics unchanged (already implemented) | Already covering missing TP/SL, API‑429, dashboard, cache, block checks | No regression | – |

**Already Implemented (no action needed)**  

- All self‑heal rules (missing TP/SL repair, API‑429 handling, dashboard restart, cache refresh, block‑on‑open‑position checks).  
- Tight stop‑loss logic (≈ 1 %).  
- Default TP = 2.5 % (will be overridden by new `OWL_TP_PCT`).  

**Rejected Proposals (with proof)**  

- **Increase position size on symbols with any loss** – contradicts the core doctrine that “big winners must outweigh many small losers”; also flagged by risk manager.  
- **Remove all block checks** – would cause repeated order rejections and potential over‑exposure; self‑heal already handles safely.  
- **Set TP to 2 % (lower than current)** – reduces reward‑to‑risk below the required 4:1, directly opposing the profit‑maximizing goal.

```json
      "idea": "Increase position size on symbols with any loss",
      "reason": "Violates profit doctrine; risk manager flags; would increase exposure without asymmetric upside"
    },
    {
      "idea": "Remove all block checks",
      "reason": "Leads to repeated order rejections and over‑exposure; self‑heal already handles safely"
    },
    {
      "idea": "Set TP to 2% (lower than current)",
      "reason": "Reduces reward‑to‑risk below required 4:1, contrary to profit‑maximizing goal"
    }
  ]
}
```

---  
**Next Steps** (for the next loop, if needed)

1. Deploy the new environment variables and verify that new trades use TP ≈ 7 % and SL ≈ 1.1 %.  
2. Run `blofin_rank_opportunities` with the new filters and confirm that the top‑ranked symbols satisfy the 24 h change and volume criteria.  
3. Monitor the first few trades to ensure the reward‑to‑risk ratio meets the ≥ 4:1 target and that no blocked orders occur.  

### End of Loop 1

### Profit-Strategist-Agent — 2026-07-01T18:02:11.206023

**Summary of Trade‑Insights Output (latest loop)**  

**1. Core Strategy Reminder**  
- **Goal:** “Big winners pay for small losers.”  
- **Priorities:**  
  - Target symbols with **high avg_win** and **high total_pnl** (big past winners).  
  - **Avoid** symbols that have accumulated **3+ losses** (repeat losers).  
  - Never clip a winning trade early; let the TP run to the full target.  

**2. Symbol‑Level Performance (key numbers)**  

| Symbol | Trades | Wins | Losses | Blocked | Total PnL | Avg Loss | Status |
|--------|--------|------|--------|---------|-----------|----------|--------|

| **DRIFT‑USDT** | 0 | 0 | 1 | 5 | **‑0.0376** | 0.0376 | *Blocked repeatedly – avoid* |
| **BTW‑USDT** | 1 | 0 | 2 | 0 | **‑0.0173** | 0.00865 | *High loss per trade* |

| **UB‑USDT** | 2 | 0 | 2 | 2 | **‑0.00971** | 0.00486 | *Blocked & losing* |
| **XAI‑USDT** | 15 | 0 | 2 | 10 | **‑0.00117** | 0.00059 | *Many blocks, no wins* |

**Key take‑aways**

- **No symbol has recorded a winning trade yet.** All win counts are zero.  
- The **largest cumulative losses** come from **RESOLV‑USDT**, **DRIFT‑USDT**, **BTW‑USDT**, **GUN‑USDT**, and **UB‑USDT** – these should be **removed from the candidate pool**.  
- **High‑block symbols** (XAI‑USDT, UB‑USDT, Q‑USDT, POPCAT‑USDT, etc.) are repeatedly rejected; they waste cycle time and should be deprioritized.  
- **Potentially usable symbols** with zero loss and no blocks: **GOAT‑USDT**, **VELVET‑USDT**, **ADA‑USDT**, **STABLE‑USDT**, **BAS‑USDT** – but they have **no trade history**; they need fresh scouting for explosive 24‑h moves.  

**3. Recent Event Log (most recent actions)**  

- **Closed losing positions:** GWEI, AIGENSYN, MON, JUP, WLD (both closes) – all realized losses ranging from ‑0.00006 to ‑0.00217.  
- **Orders placed (and blocked):**  
  - Placed BUY on **GOAT‑USDT** (size 1, TP 0.01460, SL 0.01360).  
  - Attempted BUY on **ADA‑USDT** (blocked – already long).  
  - Placed SELL on **STABLE‑USDT** (size 1, TP 0.03227, SL 0.03474).  
  - Placed SELL on **WLD‑USDT** (size 1, TP 0.3473, SL 0.3739) – later blocked because a short already existed.  
  - Placed SELL on **BAS‑USDT** (size 1, TP 0.03806, SL 0.04149).  

**4. Immediate Action Recommendations**  

| Recommendation | Reason | Expected Impact |
|----------------|--------|-----------------|
| **Remove heavy‑loss symbols** (RESOLV, DRIFT, BTW, GUN, UB, PUMP, BLESS, etc.) from the universe scan. | They contribute large negative PnL and consume margin. | Reduces margin drag, improves win‑potential pool. |
| **Blacklist repeatedly blocked symbols** (XAI, Q, POPCAT, etc.) until a change in market conditions. | Blocks waste cycle time and indicate over‑exposure or position‑mode conflicts. | Faster candidate selection, fewer order‑blocked events. |
| **Prioritize fresh candidates with zero loss & no blocks** (GOAT, VELVET, ADA, STABLE, BAS). | They have clean histories; we can test them for explosive 24 h moves. | Opens chance for first big winner, aligns with “chase past big winners”. |
| **Increase minimum 24‑h price change filter** (e.g., |chg24h| > 5 %) for new picks to ensure enough volatility for 5‑10 % targets. | Improves asymmetry – larger upside potential. | Higher expected reward per trade. |
| **Tighten stop‑loss to 1.0 %** (if not already) and set TP at **5‑10 %** for any new entry. | Enforces profit doctrine (small loss, large win). | Improves R:R toward 5:1+. |
| **Add a “no‑open‑position” guard** before placing orders (already in place, but reinforce). | Prevents duplicate long/short rejections like ADA and WLD. | Reduces order‑blocked events. |

**5. Errors / Issues Highlighted**  

- **Order blocked** for ADA‑USDT and WLD‑USDT because a position already existed – indicates the “position‑mode = net” guard missed the open‑position check.  
- **High block counts** on several symbols (e.g., Q‑USDT blocked 11 times) – suggests the universe filter is too permissive or the risk engine is rejecting due to leverage/size limits.  

**Overall Insight**  
The account is currently in a **loss‑only phase** with many symbols generating small, consistent losses and a few being repeatedly blocked. To move toward the required asymmetric payoff, the system must **prune the losing/blocked symbols**, **focus on clean, high‑volatility candidates**, and **strictly enforce the 1 % SL / 5‑10 % TP rule**. This will set the stage for capturing a single large winner that can offset the numerous small losers.
